\DoxyCodeLine{01113\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ acts\ the\ same\ as\ the\ GCC\ \_\_attribute\_\_\ ((pure))\ directive\ and\ is}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01115\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ it\ and\ to\ take\ advantage\ of\ it\ if\ and\ when\ it\ appears\ in\ other\ compilers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01116\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01117\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ "{}pure"{}\ function\ is\ one\ that\ has\ no\ effects\ except\ its\ return\ value\ and\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01118\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ its\ return\ value\ is\ a\ function\ of\ only\ the\ function's\ parameters\ or\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01119\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ non-\/volatile\ global\ variables.\ Any\ parameter\ or\ global\ variable\ access\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01120\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ must\ be\ read-\/only.\ Loop\ optimization\ and\ subexpression\ elimination\ can\ be\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01121\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ applied\ to\ such\ functions.\ A\ common\ example\ is\ strlen():\ Given\ identical\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01122\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ inputs,\ the\ function's\ return\ value\ (its\ only\ effect)\ is\ invariant\ across\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01123\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ multiple\ invocations\ and\ thus\ can\ be\ pulled\ out\ of\ a\ loop\ and\ called\ but\ once.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01124\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01125\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Example\ usage:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01126\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ EA\_PURE\ void\ Function();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01127\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01858\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ is\ a\ wrapper\ for\ the\ \#pragma\ once\ preprocessor\ directive.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01859\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ It\ allows\ for\ some\ compilers\ (in\ particular\ VC++)\ to\ implement\ signifcantly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01860\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ faster\ include\ file\ preprocessing.\ \#pragma\ once\ can\ be\ used\ to\ replace\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01861\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ header\ include\ guards\ or\ to\ augment\ them.\ However,\ \#pragma\ once\ isn't\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01862\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ necessarily\ supported\ by\ all\ compilers\ and\ isn't\ guaranteed\ to\ be\ so\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01863\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ future,\ so\ using\ \#pragma\ once\ to\ replace\ traditional\ include\ guards\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01864\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ not\ strictly\ portable.\ Note\ that\ a\ direct\ \#define\ for\ \#pragma\ once\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01865\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ impossible\ with\ VC++,\ due\ to\ limitations,\ but\ can\ be\ done\ with\ other\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01866\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ compilers/preprocessors\ via\ \_Pragma("{}once"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01867\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{01868\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Example\ usage\ (which\ includes\ traditional\ header\ guards\ for\ portability):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01869\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \#ifndef\ SOMEPACKAGE\_SOMEHEADER\_H}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01870\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \#define\ SOMEPACKAGE\_SOMEHEADER\_H}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01871\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01874\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01875\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01877\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02479\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ you\ are\ compiling\ with\ /W4\ and\ /Wall.\ There\ is\ no\ resolution\ but}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02481\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ code\ like\ this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02482\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ EA\_DISABLE\_VC\_WARNING(4625\ 4626)}}
